$('.BA-ctag1now').filter('[id^="gnn_"]').attr('className','');
$('#gnn_'+who).attr('className','BA-ctag1now');
if( 'show' != who && 1 == gnnshowing ){
$('#gnn_show').attr('className','show');
}
gnnwho = who;
gnnwhoflag = setTimeout(function(){ gnnwhoc=1; }, 200);
}
</script>

}

function fBoxRefresh() {
var scrollbarTop = window.pageYOffset || document.documentElement.scrollTop || document.body.scrollTop || 0;
var scrollbarLeft = window.pageXOffset || document.documentElement.scrollLeft|| document.body.scrollLeft || 0;
var contxClientWidth = document.documentElement.clientWidth || document.body.clientWidth || 0;
var contxClientHeight = document.documentElement.clientHeight || document.body.clientHeight || 0;
var fBox_Height = document.getElementById('flyRightBox').offsetHeight;
var fBox_remnants = contxClientHeight - fBox_Height;
if( scrollbarTop > (fBox_Height-contxClientHeight+egg('.BA-center').pos().y) && 0 >= fBox_remnants ){
fBox_style.position = 'fixed';
fBox_style.top = fBox_remnants - 5 + 'px';
fBox_style.left = fBox_posX + 'px';
if( scrollbarLeft ){
fBox_style.left = fBox_posX - scrollbarLeft + 'px';
}
}else if( scrollbarTop > fBox_posY && 0 < fBox_remnants ){
fBox_style.position = 'fixed';
fBox_style.top = '0px';
fBox_style.left = fBox_posX + 'px';
if( scrollbarLeft ){
fBox_style.left = fBox_posX - scrollbarLeft + 'px';
}
}else{
fBox_style.position = '';
}
}
function fBoxResize() {
fBox_style.position = '';
fBox_posX = egg('#flyRightBox').pos().x;
fBoxRefresh();
}
if( document.getElementById('BA-center-id').offsetHeight > document.getElementById('flyRightBox').offsetHeight ){
var fBox_posX = egg('#flyRightBox').pos().x;
var fBox_posY = egg('#flyRightBox').pos().y;
var fBox_style = document.getElementById("flyRightBox").style;
window.onscroll = fBoxRefresh;
window.onresize = fBoxResize;
}

}
}, 1500);
}

}
});
